as-block:       AS24988 - AS25162
descr:          RIPE NCC ASN block
remarks:        These AS Numbers are assigned to network operators in the RIPE NCC service region.
mnt-by:         RIPE-NCC-HM-MNT
created:        2010-05-11T11:46:03Z
last-modified:  2014-02-24T13:15:17Z
source:         RIPE

aut-num:        AS25152
as-name:        K-ROOT-SERVER
descr:          Reseaux IP Europeens Network Coordination Centre (RIPE NCC)
descr:          Originates prefixes of k.root-servers.net (root name server)
org:            ORG-RIEN1-RIPE
remarks:
remarks:        +--------------------------------------------------------------+
remarks:        | The RIPE NCC operates k.root-servers.net, one of the 13      |
remarks:        | Internet root name servers. The K-root service is            |
remarks:        | provided by a set of distributed server instances using      |
remarks:        | anycast. Each server instance announces prefixes out of      |
remarks:        | 193.0.14.0/23 and 2001:7FD::/32 in AS25152. A K-Root         |
remarks:        | server instance consists of a cluster of server              |
remarks:        | machines running the NSD name server software.               |
remarks:        |                                                              |
remarks:        | Support:  <kroot-ops@ripe.net>                               |
remarks:        | Peering:  <k-peering@ripe.net>                               |
remarks:        | WWW:      <http://k.root-servers.org>                        |
remarks:        |                                                              |
remarks:        +--------------------------------------------------------------+
remarks:        | AS25152 operates an open peering policy:                     |
remarks:        |                                                              |
remarks:        | We advertises only our own routes in AS25152                 |
remarks:        |                                                              |
remarks:        | We will update our aut-num object in the RIPE Whois          |
remarks:        | Database and kindly request you to update yours              |
remarks:        |                                                              |
remarks:        | We like to secure peering session with passwords             |
remarks:        |                                                              |
remarks:        | We would prefer not to enter into a peering contract         |
remarks:        |                                                              |
remarks:        | At our GLOBAL nodes we accept any routes offered             |
remarks:        | including transit. We will announce 193.0.14.0/24            |
remarks:        | and 2001:7FD::/48 as well as 193.0.14.0/23 and 2001:7FD::/32 |
remarks:        | as cover prefixes from this locations.                       |
remarks:        |                                                              |
remarks:        | At our LOCAL nodes we want to limit visibility of            |
remarks:        | advertisements and will likely use the well known            |
remarks:        | no-export BGP community, if you would like to                |
remarks:        | override this in order to advertise this route to your       |
remarks:        | downstream customers, please let us know in advance.         |
remarks:        | We will announce 193.0.14.0/24 and 2001:7FD::/48 from        |
remarks:        | this locations.                                              |
remarks:        |                                                              |
remarks:        | Additionally to above mentioned routes we might              |
remarks:        | announce so called service networks from our locations.      |
remarks:        | Please refer to the whois database information for           |
remarks:        | further details about this prefixes.                         |
remarks:        |                                                              |
remarks:        | In the event of problems due to leaked advertisements        |
remarks:        | it is our policy to shut down peerings and ask               |
remarks:        | questions later.                                             |
remarks:        |                                                              |
remarks:        | We tag our routes with BGP communities to reflect their      |
remarks:        | origin. See the table below for the entire list.             |
remarks:        |                                                              |
remarks:        | You can find all our details (IP, etc.) in our               |
remarks:        | PeeringDB record at: http://as25152.peeringdb.com            |
remarks:        |                                                              |
remarks:        +--------------------------------------------------------------+
remarks:        | Node   Location        Type   IPv6 Community Route-Set       |
remarks:        | ----   --------        ----   ---- --------- ---------       |
remarks:        | nl-ams NL, Amsterdam   Global Yes  25152:1   RS-KROOT-AMS-IX |
remarks:        | gb-lon UK, London      Global Yes  25152:2   RS-KROOT-LINX   |
remarks:        | jp-tyo JP, Tokyo       Global Yes  25152:3   RS-KROOT-TOKYO  |
remarks:        | us-mia US, Miami       Global Yes  25152:5   RS-KROOT-NAP    |
remarks:        | de-fra DE, Frankfurt   Global Yes  25152:11  RS-KROOT-DENIC  |
remarks:        | del    IN, Delhi       Local  Yes  25152:4   RS-KROOT-DELHI  |
remarks:        | bud    HU, Budapest    Local  Yes  25152:6   RS-KROOT-BIX    |
remarks:        | mxp    IT, Milan       Local  Yes  25152:7   RS-KROOT-MIX    |
remarks:        | ficix  FI, Helsinki    Local  Yes  25152:8   RS-KROOT-FICIX  |
remarks:        | rkv    IS, Reykjavik   Local  Yes  25152:9   RS-KROOT-ISNIC  |
remarks:        | poz    PL, Poznan      Local  Yes  25152:10  RS-KROOT-POZNAN |
remarks:        | gva    CH, Geneva      Local  Yes  25152:12  RS-KROOT-CERN   |
remarks:        | grnet  GR, Athens      Local  Yes  25152:13  RS-KROOT-GRNET  |
remarks:        | qtel   QA, Doha        Local  No   25152:14  RS-KROOT-QTEL   |
remarks:        | nskix  RU, Novosibirsk Local  Yes  25152:15  RS-KROOT-NSKIX  |
remarks:        | bne    AU, Brisbane    Local  Yes  25152:17  RS-KROOT-APNIC  |

remarks:        | BNE (APNIC)                                      |

                accept ANY

aut-num: AS25152 as-name: K-ROOT-SERVER descr: Reseaux IP Europeens Network Coordination Centre (RIPE NCC) descr: Originates prefixes of k.root-servers.net (root name server) org: ORG-RIEN1-RIPE remarks: remarks: +--------------------------------------------------------------+ remarks: | The RIPE NCC operates k.root-servers.net, one of the 13 | remarks: | Internet root name servers. The K-root service is | remarks: | provided by a set of distributed server instances using | remarks: | anycast. Each server instance announces prefixes out of | remarks: | 193.0.14.0/23 and 2001:7FD::/32 in AS25152. A K-Root | remarks: | server instance consists of a cluster of server | remarks: | machines running the NSD name server software. | remarks: | | remarks: | Support: <kroot-ops@ripe.net> | remarks: | Peering: <k-peering@ripe.net> | remarks: | WWW: <http://k.root-servers.org> | remarks: | | remarks: +--------------------------------------------------------------+ remarks: | AS25152 operates an open peering policy: | remarks: | | remarks: | We advertises only our own routes in AS25152 | remarks: | | remarks: | We will update our aut-num object in the RIPE Whois | remarks: | Database and kindly request you to update yours | remarks: | | remarks: | We like to secure peering session with passwords | remarks: | | remarks: | We would prefer not to enter into a peering contract | remarks: | | remarks: | At our GLOBAL nodes we accept any routes offered | remarks: | including transit. We will announce 193.0.14.0/24 | remarks: | and 2001:7FD::/48 as well as 193.0.14.0/23 and 2001:7FD::/32 | remarks: | as cover prefixes from this locations. | remarks: | | remarks: | At our LOCAL nodes we want to limit visibility of | remarks: | advertisements and will likely use the well known | remarks: | no-export BGP community, if you would like to | remarks: | override this in order to advertise this route to your | remarks: | downstream customers, please let us know in advance. | remarks: | We will announce 193.0.14.0/24 and 2001:7FD::/48 from | remarks: | this locations. | remarks: | | remarks: | Additionally to above mentioned routes we might | remarks: | announce so called service networks from our locations. | remarks: | Please refer to the whois database information for | remarks: | further details about this prefixes. | remarks: | | remarks: | In the event of problems due to leaked advertisements | remarks: | it is our policy to shut down peerings and ask | remarks: | questions later. | remarks: | | remarks: | We tag our routes with BGP communities to reflect their | remarks: | origin.
